Buster Jordan</username>
<time>1597899057694<//time><Rate>4< /Rate>< review>
I was fortunate enough to try out Mas Fuego the first time during a training session for work. We were the first customers of the day. The service was great. I ordered the three street taco meal with el pastor. It was cooked well and had tons of flavor. We also ordered the caso dip with chips and I have to say, the chips were awesome. They had a slight amount of chili powder sprinkled on top which not only made them look appetizing, but made the taste buds scream for more. Overall the experience was great. They had outdoor seating and premium food. The reason that I docked them a star was only because after drinking two soda waters, I had to use the restroom, which was difficult to say the least when the lights were off and only controlled from the back somewhere. I politely asked for them to be turned on, twice. They just seemed to forget. Other than that it was worth going back.</review>

<Pictures>None< /Pictures>< Review>
This was a surprising and pleasant find. We were wondering Pacific Commons looking for something to eat for lunch. We hadn't been to Mas Fuego before so we decided to give it a try. Asked the hostess what she recommended for lunch. We went with her suggestion and had the La Taqueria two tacos (popular). Let me tell you they were huge and stuffed with so much ingredients. A single taco could be enough for some. Don't be too concerned about the price. You get a lot of food and dishes can be shared. The place is well decorated with a large bar. I imagine this place could be a lively hot spot at night if it weren't for COVID restrictions. Definitely recommend this place if you have not tried it.< /Review>

I saw¬†Mas Fuego was opening up again for seating outdoor and I decided to check it out. The seating outside was not only great experience because of the food and drinks, but they have tons of space and tables and customers were at a good distance from one another. 1597391104444</Date>
<rating>5</rating>< review>
Wow wow wow. During this COVID time period, it's been tough to find good service, good food, good everything!

From beginning to end, the staff made our dining experience top notch. We were seated outside - 6 feet apart from any other patrons. Since it was our first time dining with Mas Fuego, our waitress - shout-out to Adriana!! - gave us some awesomely thorough recommendations.

We started off with the guac and chips (salsa was given, on the house), and the freshness of the ingredients in the guac really came through. As for mains, we ordered the carne asada burrito (it was HUGE) and the octopus (omggg soo tender, highly, highly recommended). And to finish everything off, we opted for the Chunuts (churro donuts!), which Adriana also gave to us on the house! Who doesn't love churros? Or donuts???But man o man. Churro + donuts?! Together?! Superb experience. Topped everything off with two margaritas, original and passion fruit. Loved it.

Will 100% return. 5 stars!</review>

< review>
JUST OUR STYLE ! My wife found this cafe online and the reviews were pretty darn good so we hit it for breakfast before checking out of our hotel in Pismo Beach. We parked in front of the place about 8.30am and things were a bit quiet we could see. Of course in these strange times things are not always as they seem. We walked up to the service counter to be greeted by a very friendly man who happened to be the co-owner Gennero. We found out his talented wife & co-owner Laura bakes the delicious pastries. It is a very rustic building dotted with lots of quaint and colorful accents plus a huge timber deck patio shaded with umbrellas. We ordered a Creme Br√ªl√©e Latte ( Gennero suggested it to my wife ) while I was happy with a Hazelnut Latte ( both small sizes with 2 shots ) plus 2 x Breakfast Paninos ( Eggs, Italian Dry Salami, Mozzarella, Fresh Spinach & Roasted Red Bell Peppers on an Italian bread roll ). I collected our Lattes from the service counter when they were ready. A few minutes later our Breakfast sandwiches also were ready to retrieve. We relaxed on the ever so cute patio bordered by lots of lush greenery. Our well made creamy lattes tasted very good and the Breakfast Paninos were a healthy start to our day ! We thanked Gennero for our lovely breakfast and wished him all the best for the future !<//review>

< Text>
This little coffee shop tucked away just off the highway in Arroyo Grande will surprise and delight.
The small coffee shop run by Gennaro and Laura has that small Italian coffee shop feel and matching coffee and treats to match.

The coffee is made with pride and one of my favorites is their americano. Try it without cream or sugar. Wow.

They also have a wide variety of treats and small bites. i have tried their breakfast sandwiches and left me full and happy.

They both always welcome you With a smile and warm hellos. You don‚Äôt want to miss this short jaunt off the highway for a little coffee and smiles.

Cheers and let me know how.l you liked it.</Text>

< Text>
Their Taiwanese Beef Noodle is the best in the area! Both soup and beef are full of flavor. The goat hot pot is kind of plain in comparison. My wife (Taiwan native) has tried other dishes and she likes them a lot as well, but for me the paigu fan is the dish to go for.  We added this restaurant to our regular rotation.  Five stars for sure!<//Review>

<Date>1453773523444<//Date><rate>5<//rate><user_name>Ivan Yudhi< /user_name>< Review>
A mom and pop shop serving your daily breakfast food like muffin egg sandwiches, donuts, and coffee.

I like the fact that all breakfast sandwiches are made to order and they taste delicious. They have 40 different combinations to try on, and also many varieties of donuts. They even insert the filling for their jelly donuts only when your order.

The shop is run by a couple and they're very friendly. I've noticed a trend that most patrons visiting the shop in the morning are regulars and know each other very well. You don't see too much of these kind of interactions these days.

A much better alternative if you're sick of the breakfast food they serve at junk food chains.< /Review>
